<a id="is-pullback-bottom-is-pullback-top-cube-is-equiv"></a><a id="4384" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4384" class="Function">is-pullback-bottom-is-pullback-top-cube-is-equiv</a> <a id="4433" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="7358" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7359" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7359" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7361" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7363" href="foundation.commuting-cubes.html#1161" class="Function">coherence-cube</a> <a id="7378" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6914" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="7380" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6926" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="7382" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6938" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="7384" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6950" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="7386" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7022" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="7389" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7037" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="7392" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7052" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="7395" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7067" class="Bound">k&#39;</a> <a id="7398" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7084" class="Bound">hA</a> <a id="7401" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7098" class="Bound">hB</a> <a id="7404" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7112" class="Bound">hC</a> <a id="7407" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#7126" class="Bound">hD</a>

<a id="12025" class="Comment">-- Section 15.2 Fiberwise pullbacks.</a>

<a id="12063" class="Comment">{- We show that if we have a square of families, such that the base square is
   a pullback square, then each square of fibers is a pullback square if and
   only if the square of total spaces is a pullback square. -}</a>

        <a id="24061" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24063" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#4047" class="Function">is-equiv-is-contr</a> <a id="24081" class="Symbol">_</a>

          <a id="24129" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24131" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#2046" class="Function">is-contr-total-path</a> <a id="24151" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24152" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#23033" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="24154" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#23055" class="Bound">c1</a><a id="24156" class="Symbol">))))</a>
      <a id="24167" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24169" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#23058" class="Bound">c2</a><a id="24171" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="24175" class="Comment">{- Next we show that for any commuting cube, if the bottom and top squares are
   pullback squares, then so is the square of fibers of the vertical maps in
   cube. -}</a>

<a id="24344" class="Comment">{-

square-fib-cube :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l1&#39; l2&#39; l3&#39; l4&#39; : Level}
  {A : UU l1} {B : UU l2} {C : UU l3} {D : UU l4}
  (f : A → B) (g : A → C) (h : B → D) (k : C → D)
  {A&#39; : UU l1&#39;} {B&#39; : UU l2&#39;} {C&#39; : UU l3&#39;} {D&#39; : UU l4&#39;}
  (f&#39; : A&#39; → B&#39;) (g&#39; : A&#39; → C&#39;) (h&#39; : B&#39; → D&#39;) (k&#39; : C&#39; → D&#39;)
  (hA : A&#39; → A) (hB : B&#39; → B) (hC : C&#39; → C) (hD : D&#39; → D)
  (top : (h&#39; ∘ f&#39;) ~ (k&#39; ∘ g&#39;))
  (back-left : (f ∘ hA) ~ (hB ∘ f&#39;))
  (back-right : (g ∘ hA) ~ (hC ∘ g&#39;))
  (front-left : (h ∘ hB) ~ (hD ∘ h&#39;))
  (front-right : (k ∘ hC) ~ (hD ∘ k&#39;))
  (bottom : (h ∘ f) ~ (k ∘ g)) →
  (c : coherence-cube f g h k f&#39; g&#39; h&#39; k&#39; hA hB hC hD
       top back-left back-right front-left front-right bottom) →
  (a : A) →
  ( ( tot (λ d&#39; p → p ∙ (bottom a)) ∘
      ( map-fib-cone h hD (pair hB (pair h&#39; front-left)) (f a))) ∘
    ( map-fib-cone f hB (pair hA (pair f&#39; back-left)) a)) ~
  ( ( map-fib-cone k hD (pair hC (pair k&#39; front-right)) (g a)) ∘
    ( map-fib-cone g hC (pair hA (pair g&#39; back-right)) a))
square-fib-cube f g h k f&#39; g&#39; h&#39; k&#39; hA hB hC hD
  top back-left back-right front-left front-right bottom c
  .(hA a&#39;) (pair a&#39; refl) =
  eq-pair-Σ
    ( pair
      ( top a&#39;)
      ( ( tr-id-left-subst
          ( top a&#39;)
          ( k (g (hA a&#39;)))
          ( ( ( inv (front-left (f&#39; a&#39;))) ∙
              ( ap h ((inv (back-left a&#39;)) ∙ refl))) ∙
            ( bottom (hA a&#39;)))) ∙
        ( ( ( assoc (inv (ap hD (top a&#39;))) _ (bottom (hA a&#39;))) ∙
            {!!}) ∙
          ( distributive-inv-concat (ap k (back-right a&#39;)) (front-right (g&#39; a&#39;)) ∙
            ( ( ap
                ( concat (inv (front-right (g&#39; a&#39;))) ?)
                ( inv (ap-inv k (back-right a&#39;)))) ∙
              ( ap
                ( concat (inv (front-right (g&#39; a&#39;))) ?)
                ( ap (ap k) (inv right-unit))))))))
-}</a>
</pre>
